<review>Just went today and got one of the apple pie caramel apples. I was so disappointed. The layer of caramel was is so thin that you can't even taste it. I have had these elsewhere and the caramel is thick and rich and blends so nicely with the white chocolate and cinnamon, but here it tasted like they watered down so that the caramel wouldn't stick to the apple.
I also purchased a dark chocolate peppermint Twinkie that had absolutely no peppermint flavor at all. Don't blame the Twinkie, don't over dip the not so dark chocolate or add some crushed peppermint sticks to it. This was obviously the owner who purchased the peppermint Twinkies and then resold them dipped for a massive margin. The label was hand written and not part of the RMCF menu. The cake was dry and seemed old. I hope this store does not reflect on how RMCF is now doing business.< /review>< pics>

< Review>
I'll admit. I've only been here a few times. But every time has been awful. Forget the smell, it's completely understandable that having so many animals in such a small location would result in an odor. No, that's not the awful thing about this place. The animals are all shoved into cages either too small, or forced in with way too many other animals to be comfortable. Almost every single one of them looks extremely stressed and unkempt. The place is just dirty, there are cockroaches running around everywhere. Sometimes even getting into the bird cages and who knows into what else. The owner may be knowledgeable, but he's not only rude, but he also treats people like they're idiots. No customer service and no one who works there will offer to help you unless you pretty much wave them down, and then they'll act like they're upset that your even there. If this wasn't one of the only places left in town to buy rats, I'd never have come in the first place. And I certainly won't be going back. I'd recommend going just about anywhere else. < review>
I'll admit. I've only been here a few times. But every time has been awful. Forget the smell, it's completely understandable that having so many animals in such a small location would result in an odor. No, that's not the awful thing about this place. The animals are all shoved into cages either too small, or forced in with way too many other animals to be comfortable. Almost every single one of them looks extremely stressed and unkempt. The place is just dirty, there are cockroaches running around everywhere. Sometimes even getting into the bird cages and who knows into what else. The owner may be knowledgeable, but he's not only rude, but he also treats people like they're idiots. No customer service and no one who works there will offer to help you unless you pretty much wave them down, and then they'll act like they're upset that your even there. If this wasn't one of the only places left in town to buy rats, I'd never have come in the first place. And I certainly won't be going back. I'd recommend going just about anywhere else. Forget supporting local businesses if they're going to treat you like an inconvenience for even coming into their store.< /review>

< Text>
This is a fantastic place to stop by for a quick bite and get a filling meal. There's only about 9 tables inside so I think that the restaurant probably anticipates a lot of customers taking their food to go. The dishes are prepared quite quickly and everything seemed clean. They have a great selection of sodas (not just the regular kind) and have some extra sauce if you need it on your meal. If the location was slightly better I think it would be a big hit! Next time you're in the mood for a teriyaki bowl, come try this place out.</Text>

Really good food. Good prices. Friendly staff. Neat clean facility. They offer chicken, tofu and beef Teriyaki bowls, combo bowls that add scrimp or fish, salads, types of Teriyaki burritos, and various burgers including a chicken burger. < text>
This place is small, easy to miss but inside is clean and comfortable. They have a unique selection of natural carbonated drinks, give them all a taste.  There is a small outdoor patio and this place is pet friendly.  We ordered the BBQ beef sandwich, Mac & Cheese and combo (chicken/beef) teriyaki bowl.  The BBQ sauce and seasoning used on the meat is tasty.  You can choose your level of spice from mild to spicy hot.   Both the chicken and beef tasted good but the beef had quite a bit of fat and gristle.  I would definitely recommend the chicken but Im not a fan of the beef, just to much gristle.< /text>

<rating>5<//rating><Review>Five stars for value and flexibility. If you're looking for elegant dining, look somewhere else but if you are looking for the best breakfast value in "the city in the country," this is the place to go.

The staff is very warm and friendly. Don't feel constrained by the written menu options, if you want to substitute pancakes for your toast they will let you do it. Don't forget refried beans are available to be substituted for the hashbrowns or kountry potato option and for just a dollar more you could have french fries with your breakfast instead.

The portions are American sized so bring your appetite. I highly recommend the breakfast quesadilla, it will fill your entire plate and even the hungriest tummy. My wife would advise to get the hash-brown tower or to go off script by customizing any of the menu options to your liking.
